add_namespace = fengtian_events
add_namespace = fengtian_political_events
add_namespace = fengtian_system_events
add_namespace = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events
add_namespace = fengtian_endgame_events

#################################
### Fengtian Political Events ###
#################################

country_event = { #Rumors incite Regionalist Uproar
	id = fengtian_events.1
	title = fengtian_events.1.t
	desc = fengtian_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_official_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.1 option fengtian_events.1.a"
		name = fengtian_events.1.a
		add_political_power = -20
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Sentiment
			add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.3 days = 16 }
			set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
}

####Suppress Regionalist Sentiment events###
country_event = { #Protests Continue REPEATING
	id = fengtian_events.3
	title = fengtian_events.3.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.3.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.3.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.3.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.3.d4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		}
	}

	option = { #Unfortunate but necessary
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.3 option fengtian_events.3.a"
		name = fengtian_events.3.a
		add_political_power = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_1
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.7 days = 25 } # An Offer from the Kenpeitai
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_3
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				}
				clr_country_flag = regionalist_protest_4
				set_country_flag = regionalist_protest_2
			}
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.3 days = 20 random_days = 25 } # Repeating
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Agent Provocateurs in Action
	id = fengtian_events.4
	title = fengtian_events.4.t
	desc = fengtian_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_riot

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Sentiment
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
	}

	option = { #Excellent
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.4 option fengtian_events.4.a"
		name = fengtian_events.4.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.5 days = 7 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Harbin Riots
	id = fengtian_events.5
	title = fengtian_events.5.t
	desc = fengtian_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_official_announcement

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good... and bad.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.5 option fengtian_events.5.a"
		name = fengtian_events.5.a
		add_political_power = -30
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.6 days = 3 random_days = 3 }
		}
		885 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
		886 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
		714 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Mass Arrests Begin
	id = fengtian_events.6
	title = fengtian_events.6.t
	desc = fengtian_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_several_prisoners

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good riddance
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.6 option fengtian_events.6.a"
		name = fengtian_events.6.a
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
				add_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
				}
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.8 days = 18 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #An Offer from the Kempeitai
	id = fengtian_events.7
	title = fengtian_events.7.t
	desc = fengtian_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_kempeitai

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Take the deal
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.7 option fengtian_events.7.a"
		name = fengtian_events.7.a
		complete_national_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
		set_temp_variable = { CAPOP = 5 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.8 days = 18 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No thank you
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.7 option fengtian_events.7.b"
		name = fengtian_events.7.b
		add_political_power = 10
		FNG_JAP_spend_small = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Regionalists suppressed
	id = fengtian_events.8
	title = fengtian_events.8.t
	desc = fengtian_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Justify_Mass_Arrests
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Silence_Targeted_Subversives
	}

	option = { #Progress
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.8 option fengtian_events.8.a"
		name = fengtian_events.8.a
		add_political_power = 10
		set_country_flag = FNG_regionalists_suppressed
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment }
			remove_ideas = FNG_Regionalist_Resentment
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage }
			remove_ideas = FNG_Regionalist_Outrage
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Picking up the Educational Slack
	id = fengtian_events.9
	title = fengtian_events.9.t
	desc = fengtian_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_mantetsu_school

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Close the Schools
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.9 option fengtian_events.9.a"
		name = fengtian_events.9.a
		add_political_power = 100
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Educational_Vacuum
			days = 185
		}
		FNG_JAP_spend_medium = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.12 days = 12 random_days = 36 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #There is no choice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.9 option fengtian_events.9.b"
		name = fengtian_events.9.b
		add_political_power = -30
		add_war_support = -0.03
		set_country_flag = school_open
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.10 days = 150 random_days = 350 }
		}
	}
}

	id = fengtian_events.10
	title = fengtian_events.10.t
	desc = fengtian_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_schooling_kimono

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #What an embarassment!

		name = fengtian_events.10.a
		add_political_power = -40
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				add = ROOT.political_power
				has_political_power < 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.11 days = 53 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Close the Mantetsu schools!

			base = 0

				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = school_open
		add_political_power = 80
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Educational_Vacuum
			days = 125
		}
		FNG_JAP_spend_medium = yes

	}
}

country_event = { #Building Infrastructure in Liaoning
	id = fengtian_events.13
	title = fengtian_events.13.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.13.d
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.13.d_jap
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_railway_map

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Chinese Contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.13 option fengtian_events.13.a"
		name = fengtian_events.13.a
		set_temp_variable = { CCPOP = 3 }
		FNG_CCPOP = yes
		FNG_JAP_spend_medium = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian_events.19 days = 36 }
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian_events.20 days = 25 }
				}
				50 = { }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_positive_factor = 275 } #55 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_positive_factor
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Japanese Contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.13 option fengtian_events.13.b"
		name = fengtian_events.13.b
		trigger = {
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CCPOP = -3 }
		FNG_CCPOP = yes
		FNG_JAP_investment_medium = yes
		add_days_remove = {
			decision = FNG_Liaoning_Infrastructure
			days = -100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian_events.19 days = 36 }
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = fengtian_events.21 days = 25 }
				}
				45 = { }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = FNG.FNG_JAP_influence_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { FNG_concordia_negative_factor = -225 } #-45 at 20%
				add = FNG_concordia_negative_factor
			}
		}
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_chosabu_efficiency
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.60 option fengtian_events.60.e"
		name = fengtian_events.60.e
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_lar = yes }
				has_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = chosabu_decryption
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc_lar = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_chosabu_intelligence
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_chosabu_decryption
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Chosabu Intelligence 1
	id = fengtian_events.67
	title = fengtian_events.67.t
	desc = fengtian_events.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_science

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.67 option fengtian_events.67.a"
		name = fengtian_events.67.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fengtian_events.67.t
				bonus = 0.66
				uses = 1
				category = decryption_tech
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_intelligence_agency = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_crypto_strength
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_crypto_strength
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
						}
						NOT = {
							has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_training_centers
						}
					}
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_training_centers
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_decryption_boost
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Japan Declares War
	id = fengtian_events.77
	title = fengtian_events.77.t

	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.77.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_breakaway } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.77.d_breakaway
		trigger = { has_country_flag = FNG_breakaway }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_ultimatum

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;JAP WAR ON FNG"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = FNG_relations_JAP_broke
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
				leave_faction = yes
				peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
			}
			JAP = {
				every_owned_state = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = { is_ally_with = FNG }
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FNG
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = FNG
					type = annex_everything
				}
				clear_JAP_FNG_hostile_AI = yes
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

		}
	}

		name = fengtian_events.78.a
		ai_chance = { base = 55 }
		add_political_power = -200
		FNG_JAP_investment_mega = yes
		add_ideas = FNG_The_Kwantung_Army
		JAP = { clear_JAP_FNG_hostile_AI = yes }
	}

	option = { #Then we strike!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.78 option fengtian_events.78.b"
		name = fengtian_events.78.b
		ai_chance = { base = 45 }
		set_global_flag = FNG_relations_JAP_broke
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
			leave_faction = yes
			peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
		}
		JAP = {
			clear_JAP_FNG_hostile_AI = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FNG
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FNG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		FNG_CA_remove = yes
		FNG_mantetsu_collapse = yes
	}
}

			NOT = {

				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.91.d_mantetsu
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
				FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_China_five_colour_flags

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.91 option fengtian_events.91.a"
		name = fengtian_events.91.a
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes }
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes }
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_medium = yes }
			add_political_power = 30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_low = yes }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_mantetsu_level_none = yes }
			add_political_power = 80
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

				has_completed_focus = FNG_Expand_the_Shenyang_Arsenal
			}
			add_political_power = 10
			add_to_variable = {
				var = prince_impress_level
				value = 1
				tooltip = FNG_impressed_prince
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prince_poisoned
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.148 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = prince_poisoned
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.144 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 70 }
	}

	option = { #The visit must be cancelled for his safety
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.143 option fengtian_events.143.b"
		name = fengtian_events.143.b
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
		}
		clr_country_flag = FNG_prince_visit
		hidden_effect = {
			FNG_close_FNG_Preparing_For_The_Princes_Visit = yes
			JAP = { country_event = { id = japan_fengtian_events.6 days = 2 } }
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		FNG_JAP_spend_medium = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
	}

	option = { #Goodbye to Prince Kan'in!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.143 option fengtian_events.143.c"
		name = fengtian_events.143.c
		trigger = {

		}

		FNG_JAP_investment_small = yes
		clr_country_flag = FNG_prince_visit

			FNG_close_FNG_Preparing_For_The_Princes_Visit = yes

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = fengtian_events.144.a

country_event = { #Prince Kan'in returns to Japan
	id = fengtian_events.147
	title = fengtian_events.147.t
	desc = fengtian_events.147.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_prince_kanin_kotohito_train_2

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { prince_impress_level < 4 } }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				JAP = { country_event = { id = japan_fengtian_events.9 days = 2 } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { FNG_prince_faith_increase = 28 }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				JAP = { country_event = { id = japan_fengtian_events.8 days = 2 } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { FNG_prince_faith_increase = 14 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { FNG_prince_faith_increase = prince_impress_level }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Hopefully they are positive
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.147 option fengtian_events.147.a"
		name = fengtian_events.147.a
		clr_country_flag = FNG_prince_visit
		hidden_effect = { FNG_close_FNG_Preparing_For_The_Princes_Visit = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_prince_impress_increase_faith
		clear_variable = prince_impress_level
	}
}

	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.1477 option fengtian_events.1477.a"

		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = motorized_equipment
			amount = 60
			producer = JAP
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_tank_chassis
			amount = 240
			producer = JAP
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Dongbei Tejian"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = light_armor ICON = GFX_unit_light_armor_icon_small COUNT = 4 }
				LINE_2 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = motorized ICON = GFX_unit_motorized_icon_small COUNT = 2 }
				SUPPORT_1 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = mot_recon ICON = GFX_unit_mot_recon_icon_small }
				SUPPORT_2 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = engineer ICON = GFX_unit_engineer_icon_small }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Dongbei Tejian" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Dongbei Tejian" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Dongbei Tejian"
				regiments = {
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					light_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					light_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					mot_recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_unit
					TYPE = "Dongbei Tejian"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Dongbei Tejian\" division_template = \"Dongbei Tejian\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
					prioritize_location = 1150
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						NOT = { controls_state = 608 } #Beijing

			}

country_event = { #Zongchang and Anqing prevent war hidden prep event, triggered by league_war.15
	id = fengtian_events.212
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_started
		SHD = { #Zongchang controls at least one 5P state
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_shandong = no }
				FNG = { add_to_array = { SHD_owned_league_states = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #checks if a proper state exists, if it does than indeed SHD owns 5P states
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = SHD_owned_league_states
					is_owned_by = SHD
				}
			}

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = SHD_owned_league_states
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { state = 1047 }
						NOT = { state = 598 }
						NOT = { state = 1075 }
					}
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SHD_owned_crit_anq_states = PREV } }
				}
				else = {
					FNG = { add_to_array = { SHD_owned_jiangsu_states = PREV } }
				}
			}

			if = { #checks if a proper state exis, if yes than SHD owns 5P states crit by ANQ
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = SHD_owned_crit_anq_states
						is_owned_by = SHD
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_controls_5p_crit_state
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_jiangsu
				SHD = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								controls_state = 1047
								controls_state = 598
								controls_state = 1075
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1047 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SHD_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1047.id } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 598 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SHD_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 598.id } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { controls_state = 1075 }
							}
							FNG = {
								set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
								add_to_array = { SHD_nonowned_jiangsu_states = 1075.id } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong
		}

		country_event = { id = fengtian_events.213 days = 1 }
	}
}

				add = 100
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_controls_5p_crit_state
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_ANQ }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_SHD }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_NOONE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_PEACE }

					has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin's Proposal Accepted
	id = fengtian_events.221
	title = fengtian_events.221.t
	desc = fengtian_events.221.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.221 option fengtian_events.221.a"
		name = fengtian_events.221.a
		set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_paccepted
		ANQ = {
			country_event = { id = anqing_events.132 days = 1 }
		}
		SHD = {
			country_event = { id = shandong_events.36 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ANQ = { has_country_flag = ANQ_lep_beat_chi } }
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.225 days = 14 }
			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = anqing_events.136 days = 11 }
			}
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.40 days = 11 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SHD_owned_league_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_keepjiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_jiangsu }
			}
			ANQ = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = FNG.SHD_owned_crit_anq_states
					transfer_state = v
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_getjiangsu
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu } }
				SHD = {
					for_each_loop = {
						array = FNG.SHD_nonowned_jiangsu_states
						transfer_state = v
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				SHD = {
					for_each_loop = {
						array = FNG.SHD_nonowned_jiangsu_states
						transfer_state = v
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin's Proposal Rejected
	id = fengtian_events.222
	title = fengtian_events.222.t
	desc = fengtian_events.222.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.222 option fengtian_events.222.a"
		name = fengtian_events.222.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_inshandong
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, anq offers but fengtian doesnt
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_inshandong
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqall5p }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong }
			}
			#all situations but shandong having only shandong
			#if they have critical part, they keep all of jiangsu
			#if they have jiangsu parts, they keep those parts
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_controls_5p_crit_state
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			}
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHDwantjiangsu }
			}
			#shandong part jiangsu, doesnt need rest jiangsu
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_getjiangsu
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong
			}
			#shandong only shandong, if anq is willing get all jiangsu, if not only xuzhou potent
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqgivejiangsu
				}
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_getxuzhou
			}
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_everything
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHDkeepall }
			}
			#shandong controls a crit state, but is actually willing to give up
			set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.37 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = anqing_events.131 days = 1 }
			}
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = shandong_events.35 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					tag = ANQ

					tag = SHD

						OR = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrzhang
							has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrchen

					}
				}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30

				add = 20
				tag = ANQ

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				tag = SHD
				FNG = {
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrzhang
					has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrchen
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_ANQ }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_SHD }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_NOONE }

			}
		}

						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno }

					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				FNG = {
					set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDyes
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqyes }
						country_event = { id = fengtian_events.233 days = 1 }

					else_if = {

					}
				}
			}

					if = {

						country_event = { id = fengtian_events.234 days = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {

						country_event = { id = fengtian_events.234 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {

					set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno

		trigger = { tag = ANQ }

	desc = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.231 option fengtian_events.231.a"

			limit = { tag = ANQ }

				declare_war_on = {
					target = ANQ
					type = annex_everything

country_event = { # The Compromise is Accepted
	id = fengtian_events.233
	title = fengtian_events.233.t
	desc = fengtian_events.233.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.233 option fengtian_events.233.a"
		name = fengtian_events.233.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FNG }
			give_guarantee = SHD
			if = {
				limit = { 1047 = { is_controlled_by = SHD } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1047 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 598 = { is_controlled_by = SHD } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 598 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 1075 = { is_controlled_by = SHD } }
				ANQ = { transfer_state = 1075 }
			}

			ANQ = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.233 days = 1 }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = anqing_events.64 days = 4 }
					remove_targeted_decision = { decision = ANQ_attack_SHD target = SHD }
				}

				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SHD state = 1047 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SHD state = 598 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = SHD state = 1075 }
			}
			SHD = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.233 days = 1 }
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_targeted_decision = { decision = SHD_intervene_southeast target = ANQ }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1047.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 598.building_level@industrial_complex }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories = 1075.building_level@industrial_complex }

				set_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 1047.building_level@arms_factory }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 598.building_level@arms_factory }
				add_to_temp_variable = { SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories = 1075.building_level@arms_factory }

				add_offsite_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_civ_factories
				}
				add_offsite_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = SHD_jiangsu_exploitation_mil_factories
				}
			}

			1047 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			598 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			1075 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ANQ_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			597 = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SHD_jiangsu_shandong_deal_dynamic_modifier }
			}

			set_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_success
			hidden_effect = { country_event = league_war.18 }
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqall5p
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqgivejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqtheykeepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_anqthreatzhang
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_first_demands_heard
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_anqcedejiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_cedenonjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_getxuzhou
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_ideal_keepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_p1_anqno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_p1_anqyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_p1_SHDno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_p1_SHDyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_everything
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_getjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_inshandong
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_shd_keepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_controls_5p_crit_state
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_notall_jiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_jiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHD_only_shandong
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHDkeepall
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHDkeepjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc_SHDwantjiangsu
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqyes
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrchen
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_specrzhang
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_split
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
			clr_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDyes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ANQ }
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ANQ_reclamation_willingness
				value = 1
				tooltip = ANQ_increase_reclamation_war_willingness_tt
			}

		}
	}

			has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.234.d2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
			NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.234.d3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
			has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_SHD_zhang_zongchang_coat_1

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #no stance choice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.234 option fengtian_events.234.a"
		name = fengtian_events.234.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno }
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno }
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_ANQ }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_SHD }
				}
			}
		}
		ANQ = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.232 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.237 days = 5 }
		}
		SHD = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.232 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.237 days = 5 }
		}
	}

	option = { #support chen choice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.234 option fengtian_events.234.b"
		name = fengtian_events.234.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno }
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno }
				add = -20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_SHD }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_NOONE }
				}
			}
		}

		ANQ = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.232 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = anqing_events.134 days = 5 }
		}
		SHD = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.232 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = shandong_events.39 days = 5 }
		}
	}

	option = { #support zhang choice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.234 option fengtian_events.234.c"
		name = fengtian_events.234.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
				add = -30
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno }
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_anqno
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FNG_anqSHD_warc2_SHDno }
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_ANQ }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ANQ_deal option = ANQ_DEAL_WAR_NOONE }
				}
			}
		}
		ANQ = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.232 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = anqing_events.135 days = 5 }

			NOT = { has_war_with = QIE }
		}

				has_idea = FNG_ANQ_Reconstruction_Plan

		}
	}

			}
			modifier = {

					ratio < 0.7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.6
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = FROM.num_of_factories }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = ROOT.num_of_factories }
				divide_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = -3 }
				add = FNG_japan_accept_chance
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = FNG_breakaway
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.77 days = 4 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.285 option fengtian_events.285.b"
		name = fengtian_events.285.b #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.7
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.6
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = FROM.num_of_factories }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = ROOT.num_of_factories }
				divide_temp_variable = { FNG_japan_accept_chance = 3 }
				add = FNG_japan_accept_chance
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = JAP
							is_core_china = yes
						}
						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = JAP
								owner = { is_subject_of = JAP }
							}
							is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = FNG
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FNG = { has_idea = unequal_treaties_japan } }
				FNG = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = unequal_treaties_japan
						add_idea = free_trade
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.286 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LEC = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
			}

		}
	}

country_event = { # Fengtian Requests Assistance with Bandits Again
	id = fengtian_events.316
	title = fengtian_events.316.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.316.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_JAP_bandit_clash
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_events.316.d_clash #Option fengtian_events.316.a is disabled to prevent a repeat of fengtian_events.313
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = FNG_JAP_bandit_clash
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_honghuzi

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FNG_JAP_hostile = no
		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

	option = { #Deploy the Railway Guard
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.316 option fengtian_events.316.a"
		name = fengtian_events.316.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_JAP_bandit_clash #Deactivated to prevent a repeat of fengtian_events.313
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 15
		add_manpower = -15000
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # Arisaka Type 38 ~1918
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = -300
			producer = JAP
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # ~1934
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = -50
			producer = JAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe
				amount = -3
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = small_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = -6
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.311 hours = 8 }
			FNG_JAP_investment_medium = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
	}

	option = { #Provide weapons and reconnaissance (Reduces expedition cost for FNG)
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.316 option fengtian_events.316.b"
		name = fengtian_events.316.b
		add_political_power = 5
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { # Arisaka Type 38 ~1918
			type = infantry_equipment_0
			amount = -100
			producer = JAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe
				amount = -3
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_design_based_on = small_plane_airframe }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = -6
				producer = JAP
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.314 hours = 8 }
			FNG_JAP_investment_small = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 45 }
	}

	option = { #This is beneath us
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_events.316 option fengtian_events.316.c"
		name = fengtian_events.316.c
		FNG = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_events.313 hours = 8 }
			FNG_JAP_spend_small = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
	}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
							has_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
						}
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_radar_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_construction_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_efficiency_event_2
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_1
				clr_country_flag = FNG_chosabu_decryption_event_2
				#break = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = fengtian_system_events.7 days = 20 random_days = 5 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Radar

			has_country_flag = chosabu_radar
		}
		country_event = fengtian_system_events.8

country_event = { #Clear out railway variables
	id = fengtian_system_events.14
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		check_variable = { FNG_mantetsu_rails < 3 }
		check_variable = { FNG_national_rails < 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { FNG_rail_decisions_taken = FNG_mantetsu_rails }
		add_to_temp_variable = { FNG_rail_decisions_taken = FNG_national_rails }
		check_variable = { FNG_rail_decisions_taken > 2 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_system_events.14 option 1"
		clear_variable = FNG_mantetsu_rails
		clear_variable = FNG_national_rails
	}
}

country_event = { #Encryption Codes Leaked!
	id = fengtian_political_events.15
	title = fengtian_political_events.15.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.15.d_Ruan
		trigger = {
			FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.15.d_Wang
		trigger = {
			FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.15.d_Tang
		trigger = {
			FNG_tang_yulin = { is_character = event_target:leaker }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_harbin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FNG_encryption_codes_leaked
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			FNG_wang_yintai = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
		else = {
			FNG_tang_yulin = { save_event_target_as = leaker }
		}
	}

	option = { #Damn!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_political_events.15 option fengtian_political_events.15.a"
		name = fengtian_political_events.15.a
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		add_political_power = -20
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Intel_Leak
			days = 60
		}
		if = { #It's Ruan Zhenduo
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			FNG_JAP_investment_medium = yes
		}
		else_if = { #It's Wang Yintai
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
			FNG_JAP_investment_small = yes
		}
		else = { #It's Tang Yulin
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			FNG_JAP_investment_small = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Remove him from office!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_political_events.15 option fengtian_political_events.15.b"
		name = fengtian_political_events.15.b
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FNG_Intel_Leak
			days = 60
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FNG_ruan_zhenduo = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			FNG_JAP_spend_medium = yes
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = 3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
			deactivate_advisor = FNG_ruan_zhenduo_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_japan_dislike
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FNG_wang_yintai = { is_character = event_target:leaker } }
			set_temp_variable = { RLPOP = -3 }
			FNG_RLPOP = yes
			deactivate_advisor = FNG_wang_yintai_advisor
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ZCPOP = -3 }
			FNG_ZCPOP = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { JAP = { is_ai = no } }
				JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { QIE = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						is_ai = no
					}
					country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { LEC = { is_ai = no } }
				QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 } }
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china
								JAP = { is_faction_leader = no }
							}
						}
						JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								NOT = { country_exists = LEC }
								LEC = { is_in_faction = yes }
								LEC = { is_subject = yes }
							}
						}
						LEC = { country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 } }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = no
						}
						random_enemy_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_war = yes
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT }
							country_event = { id = fengtian_events.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = no
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.28.t.major
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.28.d.minor
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = no
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_political_events.28.d.major
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value
			value < 6
		}
		OR = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_high = yes
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value
					value = 5
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = fengtian_events.321 hours = 66 } #An End to the Protests
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_political_events.28 option fengtian_political_events.28.a"
		name = fengtian_political_events.28.a
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = no
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_projapan
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value value = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_political_events.28 option fengtian_political_events.28.a"
		name = fengtian_political_events.28.a
		trigger = {
			FNG_mantetsu_level_very_high = yes
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = FNG_projapan
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = FNG_mantetsu_protest_value value = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Tensions in Manchuria
	id = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002
	title = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002.t
	desc = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_revolt

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [ON ACTION] on_war_relation_added

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = yes
	show_major = {
		OR = {
			is_tag_in_china_area = yes
			original_tag = JAP
			original_tag = GEA
			any_home_area_neighbor_country = {
				is_tag_in_china_area = yes
				is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { FNG_JAP_hostile = yes }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002 option fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002.a"
		name = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002.a #When you play the game of thrones, you win or you die.
		custom_effect_tooltip = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.002.tt #Warn everyone what will happen if Zhang fails to win
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FNG }
			#Do these both FNG side so they are synched
			activate_mission = FNG_japanese_patience_runs_thin_mission
			hidden_effect = {
				JAP = {
					activate_mission = JAP_faith_in_zhang_runs_out_mission
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_variable = FNG_prince_faith_increase
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = FNG_japanese_patience_runs_thin_mission
						days = FNG_prince_faith_increase
					}
					JAP = {
						add_days_mission_timeout = {
							mission = JAP_faith_in_zhang_runs_out_mission
							days = FNG.FNG_prince_faith_increase
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = JAP }
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = JAP_faith_in_zhang_runs_out_mission }
		}
	}
}

	title = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.t
	desc = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_parade_shanghai

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] ai_events.205 // SSJW War Ai Event and FNG has active mission FNG_japanese_patience_runs_thin_mission

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030 option fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.a"
		name = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.a #At least this way we ensure China will have a voice in the sphere.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = FNG_japanese_patience_runs_thin_mission }
			remove_mission = FNG_japanese_patience_runs_thin_mission
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = { add_to_faction = FNG }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.032 days = 1 } } #[FNG.GetNameDefCap] Joins the Sphere
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;FNG TENSIONS IN MANCHURIA - Japan Enters the Fray, Fengtian Joins the CPS"
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030 option fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.b"
		name = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.030.b #Please, we just need some more time to sort out our affairs
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FNG_JAP_mech_sub_time_mega_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian_japan_mechanic_events.033 days = 1 } } #[FNG.GetNameDefCap] Stalls for Time
		}
	}
}

#FNG - Endgame Events

country_event = { #
	id = fengtian_endgame_events.000
	title = fengtian_endgame_events.000.t
	desc = fengtian_endgame_events.000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_zhang_zuolin_new_uniform_1

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [DECISION] fengtian_endgame_events.000

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = fengtian_endgame_events.001 days = 3 }
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					is_chinese_tag = yes
					NOT = {
						tag = UPC
						tag = NPA
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = fengtian_endgame_events.004 days = 7 } #A Nation Under the Northeast
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = UPC
						tag = NPA
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = UPC.twindragonevents.005 days = 5 } #Unification On Equal Terms
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.000 option fengtian_endgame_events.000.a"
		name = fengtian_endgame_events.000.a #
	}
}

country_event = { #A Nation Under the Northeast
	id = fengtian_endgame_events.004
	title = fengtian_endgame_events.004.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_endgame_events.004.d.shd
		trigger = {
			tag = SHD
			china_is_aligned_with_fengtian = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_endgame_events.004.d.shx
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = { character = SHX_yan_xishan }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian_endgame_events.004.d.generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = SHD
					china_is_aligned_with_fengtian = yes
				}
				AND = {
					tag = SHX
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_yan_xishan }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes #[EVENT] fengtian_endgame_events.000

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.004 option fengtian_endgame_events.004.a"
		name = fengtian_endgame_events.004.a #We can't let their corruption rule us! To arms!
		#trigger = {
		#	CHN_has_civil_war_prep_trigger = yes
		#}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FNG
					ratio > 0.80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = FNG
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FNG
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { CHN_civil_war_preparation_var > 0 }
			}
		}
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is FNG
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #Beiyang
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform FNG
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = fengtian_endgame_events.005 days = 1 } #The [FROM.Adjective] Revolt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.004 option fengtian_endgame_events.004.b"
		name = fengtian_endgame_events.004.b #We welcome Marshal [FNG.GetLeader]!
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.004 option fengtian_endgame_events.004.c"
		name = fengtian_endgame_events.004.c #Let us send a delegation to the capital. (Switch to [FNG.GetNameDef])
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang }
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }
		FNG = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			FNG = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.191 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Joins Our Government
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes #[FOCUS] FNG_a_reformed_government

	option = { #Zhang Zongxiang
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.006 option 1"
		trigger = { JAP = { has_authoritarian_government = no } }
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		activate_advisor = FNG_lu_zongyu_sic
	}

	option = { #Wang Yitang
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.006 option 2"
		trigger = { JAP = { has_authoritarian_government = no } }
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		activate_advisor = FNG_jin_yunpeng_sic
	}

	option = { #Tofu
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event fengtian_endgame_events.006 option 3"
		trigger = { JAP = { has_authoritarian_government = yes } }
		promote_character = {
			character = FNG_zhang_jinghui
			ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
		}
		activate_advisor = FNG_kita_seiichi_sic
	}
}
